20.3(1): 'byams bskang ba'i rgyud la/ lha gsas gyer dang cho rabs kyi rgyud dang / stong 
20.4(1): gsum rin chen gling mdos kyi rgyud dang gnyis su 'byung ba'o/ /de dag rgyud sde chen 
20.5(1): po bcu gnyis las/ smrang chen po chu bo gzhung bzhi'i brda sbyar nas/ gto rabs 
20.6(1): shing lo rgyas par bstan pa ste/ rtsa ba'i rgyud chen sum cu rtsa gnyis la/ yan lag 
20.7(1): rgyud sde sum brgya drug cur dbye/ nying lag le'u khri dang drug stong dbye/ lo ma 'bum 
20.8(1): khri 'bum stong bshad pa la/ gto thabs bye ba sa ya bsam las 'das/ chab nag 
20.9(1): srid pa rgyud kyi bon sgo la/ zad cing 'bri med rgya mtsho mtha' yas klong / nam mkha' 
20.10(1): ri rab rgya mtsho sa gzhi ltar/ 'gro la phan bde bsod nams bskyed pa dang / gang 
20.11(1): la gang 'dul rtsis dang grangs la 'das/ phun tshogs ngo mtshar 'dod dgu 'byung 
20.12(1): ba yi/ rtsi shing nags tshal skyed mo'i tshal dang mtshungs/ de yang 'gro la phan bde 
20.13(1): bskyed pa la/ snying rje byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed cing / sems can rnams 
20.14(1): la byams pa dga' ba dang / snying rje btang snyoms rgyun du 'jug par bya/ yid 
20.15(1): gzhungs ngag 'jam bran gyi tha ma bzhin/ mig kyang sems can kun la mas yar 
20.16(1): bltas/ gsung dbyangs tshangs pa'i khu byug mgrin lta bu/ snyan la dngas shing tshangs 
20.17(1): par dbyung ba dang / ne'u tso'i gcong skad co ga'i 'gyur skad dang / mgrin bzang 
20.18(1): pho mo mtshal bu'i gsung skad dang / 'dab chags gsung snyan cho dgu'i skad bzhin

20.20(1): par/ bka' lung rig pa zung du 'brel nas su/ thabs mkhas lag len shin tu 
20.21(1): ldan par bya/ chab nag nus pa smrang dang brda yis 'phrod/ gson gshin gnyis kyang

21.2(1): can bla bzung dongs su 'gug pa dang / dbugs med gzugs la srog chags 'gro

21.11(1): dus mtha'i bar du nub mi 'gyurar/ chab nag srid pa 'gro ba'i kha lo bsgyur/ zhes

21.13(1): la bka' stsal to/ /

442.13(1): bstan 'dzin skyes chen dam pa rnams kyi sku tshe bskal brgyar brtan zhing bzhed dgongs 
442.14(1): lhun gyis 'grub pa dang / 'brel thogs kyi sbyin pa'i bdag po dang las gzhi 'di'i byed 
442.15(1): po kun tshe bsod dbang khams gong nas gong du mtho ste myur du sku gsum rdzogs pa'i 
442.16(1): sangs rgyas kyi go 'phang thob pa dang / zhang bod rig gzhung rnams mi nyams gong nas 
442.17(1): gong du 'phel te 'dzam gling tha gru yongs kyi snod bcud rgud pa gso zhing phan bde'i 
442.18(1): gsos su khyab pa dang / yangs pa'i rgyal khams kun du nad mug 'khrug rtsod dang rang 
442.19(1): byung 'byung ba'i 'jigs pa rnams rmeng med du zhi nas bde legs phun tshogs skyid kyi nyi
